In this table, the "mean" means the empirically measured average funniness score when the "unfunny", "somewhat funny" and "funny" receive a funniness score of 1, 2, 3 respectively. "Precison" is the measures the uncertainity of the empirical mean estimation; specifically, with 95% confidence the true funniness score lies in the range [μ - σ, μ + σ] for a empirically measured mean μ and precision σ.
